# Infected-Silvester
[Back to Outline](#outline)  
Lore order: (1) ''Silvester'' Is infected with the xeno virus, his gear prevents the spreading of it. how can we save him from the infection.

# Blitzkrieg
[Back to Outline](#outline)  
Lore order: (2) The machine got hacked by someone... it wants you dead.
Originally build by Kahmlstein together with Ruina and Expidonsa...
Do not fight him in any expidonsan areas...
